{\bfseries Value\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}
6  \textcolor{comment}{/* const struct retro\_message * --}
\textcolor{comment}{                                            * Sets a message to be displayed in implementation-specific
       manner }
\textcolor{comment}{                                            * for a certain amount of 'frames'.}
\textcolor{comment}{                                            * Should not be used for trivial messages, which should simply
       be }
\textcolor{comment}{                                            * logged via RETRO\_ENVIRONMENT\_GET\_LOG\_INTERFACE (or as a }
\textcolor{comment}{                                            * fallback, stderr).}
\textcolor{comment}{                                            */}
\end{DoxyCode}
